\ProblemFileHeader{XTL_SV_QUESTIONCOUNT}% Process how many problems are in this file and how to detect if it has a desirable problem
\ifproblemToFind% If it has a desirable problem search the file.
%\tagged{Ans@MultiAns, Type@Compute, Topic@Derivative, Sub@Exp, Sub@Theorems-MVT, File@0053}{
\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0053. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Does the function ${e^{\left(5 \, x\right)}}$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,{2}]$?

\input{Derivative-Compute-0053.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,{2}]$
\choice No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,{2})$
\choice No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,{2}]$
\choice[correct] Yes, all the conditions are met
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{\frac{1}{5} \, \log\left(\frac{1}{10} \, e^{10} - \frac{1}{10}\right)}\]
\end{problem}}%}

Does the function ${7 \, e^{\left(-6 \, x\right)}}$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,{1}]$?

\input{Derivative-Compute-0053.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,{1}]$
\choice No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,{1})$
\choice No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,{1}]$
\choice[correct] Yes, all the conditions are met
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{-\frac{1}{6} \, \log\left(-\frac{1}{6} \, e^{\left(-6\right)} + \frac{1}{6}\right)}\]
\end{problem}}%}

Does the function ${e^{\left(-4 \, x\right)}}$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,{3}]$?

\input{Derivative-Compute-0053.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,{3}]$
\choice No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,{3})$
\choice No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,{3}]$
\choice[correct] Yes, all the conditions are met
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{-\frac{1}{4} \, \log\left(-\frac{1}{12} \, e^{\left(-12\right)} + \frac{1}{12}\right)}\]
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,{2}]$
\choice No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,{2})$
\choice No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,{2}]$
\choice[correct] Yes, all the conditions are met
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{\frac{1}{4} \, \log\left(\frac{1}{8} \, e^{8} - \frac{1}{8}\right)}\]
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{problem}

Does the function ${-e^{\left(-x\right)}}$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,{5}]$?

\input{Derivative-Compute-0053.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,{5}]$
\choice No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,{5})$
\choice No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,{5}]$
\choice[correct] Yes, all the conditions are met
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{-\log\left(-\frac{1}{5} \, e^{\left(-5\right)} + \frac{1}{5}\right)}\]
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{problem}

Does the function ${-3 \, e^{\left(10 \, x\right)}}$ satisfy the conditions of the Mean Value Theorem (MVT) over the interval $[0,{4}]$?

\input{Derivative-Compute-0053.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice No, the function is not continuous over the closed interval $[0,{4}]$
\choice No, the function is not differentiable over the open interval $(0,{4})$
\choice No, the function is not defined over the interval $[0,{4}]$
\choice[correct] Yes, all the conditions are met
\end{multipleChoice}

If the conditions are met, then find all numbers $c$ that satisfy the conclusion of the MVT.  If the conditions are not met, then write ``NONE.''

\[c = \answer{\frac{1}{10} \, \log\left(\frac{1}{40} \, e^{40} - \frac{1}{40}\right)}\]
\end{problem}}%}
